The Situation in East Africa is Increasingly Tense, Europe is in a Precarious State; The Mediterranean Sea Becomes the Center of Military Action; Britain Actively Reinforces Defenses in Malta; Submarine Fleet Concentrates on the South Coast to Standby

The Mediterranean Sea has become the center of military operations today, second only to the Italian-Ethiopian border in East Africa. It is widely rumored that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini intends to occupy Albania with troops to protect the borders of neighboring Little Entente countries. This news, coupled with the British fleet's deployment to the Suez Canal, makes the European situation even more precarious. According to sources in Athens, Italy has recently secretly transported a large number of munitions and many military officers to the Albanian coast. (National Telegram, 29th)

(London) The British Mediterranean fleet is actively being deployed from Malta today. It is said to be a routine cruise, but in reality, this is the largest naval deployment since the precarious situation in Italy and Albania. Among them, the battleships "Revenge" and "Valiant", and the cruisers "London", "Devonshire", and "Shropshire", and the repair ship "Resource" have all sailed to Alexandria. The battleship "Resolution" and the cruiser "Emerald" have sailed to Port Said. The cruisers "Arethusa", "Delhi", and "Curlew", as well as the sloop "Godolphin", have sailed to Haifa. (National Telegram, 29th)

Malta is currently engaged in preventing possible aerial gas bomb attacks. The police have conducted gas defense drills and recruited a police reserve force to strengthen their capabilities. Dockworkers and engineers are now very active. The port defenses are more sophisticated than during the European War and are nearing completion. The system of requiring foreigners to obtain permits from the police station before landing is now being reinstated. (Special Telegram from the North-China Daily News, 29th)

Portsmouth: Malta Island is Britain's naval base in the Mediterranean. It is currently busy transporting anti-aircraft guns there. At the same time, naval mobilizations are also progressing in that direction, indicating that the British naval activity in the Mediterranean has exceeded the normal level. (National Telegram, 29th)

(Paris) A reporter dispatched by Le Matin to Italy to observe the army's large-scale maneuvers recently stated that the Italian government has ordered 60 submarines to prepare everything at the Augusta naval base in southern Sicily and has ordered the air force to concentrate in that province. The port of Augusta is quite close to the British-owned Malta Island in the Mediterranean. British authorities recently sent warships to the island. The general public believes that this move by the Italian government is directed at Britain. (Agence Havas Telegram, 30th)

(Rome) It is rumored that the government has ordered 60 submarines to prepare everything at the Augusta naval base in Sicily. Local newspapers, due to Italian laws prohibiting the publication of military news, have neither confirmed nor denied this. However, well-informed sources believe that if the government were to mobilize the submarine fleet due to the British aircraft carrier Glorious and other warships sailing to Malta, it could do so openly without concealment. Furthermore, when the cabinet met in Bolzano yesterday, it was rumored that the Italian government, due to British warships having sailed to Aden, intended to send a portion of its fleet to the Suez Canal to counter them. However, after the cabinet meeting concluded, the authorities issued a communique expressing a willingness to compromise with Britain, which contradicted the rumors. Therefore, even if the Italian government were to order its army, navy, and air force to prepare everything, it would only be for dealing with Abyssinia and would have no other intentions. (Agence Havas Telegram, 30th)

(London) Today, French and German newspapers all stated that the situation between Italy and Albania has become more precarious after the Italian cabinet held a special meeting in Bolzano. The opinion of the French authorities can be discerned from the commentary in Le Temps, which stated that the Italian government is determined to pursue its established policy, regardless of the decisions of the League of Nations Administrative Council on September 4th. This is now even more evident. According to German newspapers, the resolutions of Bolzano prove that Italy is determined to achieve its goals without the consent of the League of Nations or Britain, and may even resist both parties. However, the Rome Tribuna stated that Italy's policy does not directly or indirectly endanger British interests. (Reuters Telegram, 29th)

Britain Mobilizes Diplomatic and Military Power to Cope with Future Serious Events; Mediterranean Fleet is Busy with Mobilization; External Study to Formulate Measures

(London) Italy's provocative actions towards the world have led Britain to mobilize its army, navy, and diplomatic power to cope with serious events, namely, those warned against by Mussolini. Legal experts outside the British government are currently studying the content of the U.S. Neutrality Act signed by President Roosevelt to prepare recommendations regarding the abolition of the embargo on munitions and actions to impose sanctions on Italy in the event of war. It is not entirely clear whether the U.S. Neutrality Act also prohibits cotton, copper, steel, and chemicals. If the League of Nations and Britain impose sanctions on the aggressor, the sanctions will inevitably be ineffective if the United States does not prohibit these items. Military activity in Portsmouth is currently very intense. Anti-aircraft guns are being loaded onto the Benledi, and it is rumored that the Benledi has received secret orders to sail to Malta Island. Air Force officers and soldiers stationed at the Lee-on-the-Solent naval base have also been ordered to stand by today. (National News Agency Telegram, 30th)

Italian Cabinet Decision; No Reaction in Paris; Unwilling to Participate in Any Sanctions Against Italy

(Paris) The Italian cabinet's resolutions at the Bolzano meeting have not caused a special reaction from the French newspapers. According to most people's opinions, France is caught between two major powers. Therefore, before Britain clarifies its path at Geneva, it cannot concretely express its attitude towards the Italian-Ethiopian issue. Le Volf claims a reliable source saying Sir Eden arriving in Geneva will soon lobby most member countries behind the scenes to support financial and economic sanctions, but Eden will abandon any coercive military plans, such as blockade plans. Le Journal claims the French prime minister has clearly expressed at a recent cabinet meeting that France is unwilling to participate in any plans to sanction Italy. (National Telegram, 29th)

Italian-Ethiopian War Inevitable; Likelihood of Outbreak is Ninety-Nine to One; British Foreign Secretary Stays in London to Observe the Development of the Situation

(London) According to Exchange Telegraph, today's Athens telegram stated that garrison islands are being fortified in order to blockade the Adriatic Sea in the event of war. Lloyd's Insurance Company announced that the possibility of an Italian-Ethiopian war breaking out is 99 to 1, and the possibility of an outbreak within a month is 4 to 1. Foreign Secretary Hoare has canceled his plans to travel to Aix-les-Bains, France, in order to observe the changes in the Italian-Ethiopian situation in London. Prime Minister Baldwin is currently vacationing in Aix and will return to London on September 4th. (National Telegram, 29th)

League of Nations Faces Difficulties in Handling the Italian-Ethiopian Dispute; Will it Follow the Precedent of the Sino-Japanese Case and Regard Delay as the Best Policy?

(Paris) Renowned reporter Pertinax recently published an article in Le Petit Parisien, predicting the procedures that the League of Nations Administrative Council may take when discussing the Italian-Ethiopian dispute on September 4th. It is said that "During the Administrative Council meeting, the British representative will submit a report. The impact of this report on Italy and other member states of the Administrative Council will largely depend on its wording and manner of presentation." Once the British report is submitted, the Italian representative will officially read out the documents accusing Ethiopia. The Administrative Council will consider it necessary to review each of the accusations and will invoke Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant to conduct an investigation in order to draft a report. Because the procedures outlined in this article are very complicated, they cannot be completed in a short period of time. The Italian-Ethiopian dispute can thus be delayed, and the talks that were interrupted halfway through the Paris Conference can continue to be held by Britain, France, Italy, and Ethiopia. The Administrative Council may even follow the precedent of the Manchurian dispute, appointing a commission to conduct an on-site investigation in Ethiopia in order to submit a report. "This delaying tactic is commonly used by the League of Nations to handle thorny issues, but whether the member states of the current Administrative Council will obey orders is still uncertain. Because Britain advocates strict adherence to the Covenant, there will be no shortage of supporters in the Administrative Council. The Chairman of the Administrative Council, namely the Argentine representative Quenaz, as well as the representatives of Mexico and Chile, will definitely support the British proposal." Other countries such as Spain, Portugal, and Denmark will also advocate this, but the attitude of other member states is still difficult to predict, and there may be entanglements during the Administrative Council meeting, so it is not necessarily certain what kind of measures will be decided. (Agence Havas Telegram, 30th)

Cecil Criticizes Italian Actions

(London) Renowned international peace activist and League of Nations advocate Viscount Cecil told a reporter from the Associated Press today that Italy's aggression against Ethiopia, regardless of the pretext, will ultimately drag civilized nations into the vortex of war. All civilized countries must find ways to prevent the Italian-Ethiopian war. Cecil also strongly advocated the League of Nations' sanctions against Italy. Assuming that powerful countries can bully the weak with their military force without any constraints, how can small countries have faith in so-called "civilization"? (National Telegram, 29th)

Italy Deploys National Forces to Cope with East African War; Youths Over Seventeen Must Receive Military Training; European Laborers Prepare for Anti-Italian General Strike

Three more troop transports carrying 6,000 Blackshirts will depart for East Africa today and tomorrow. Another group will depart on September 1st. The number of volunteers heading to East Africa has recently increased significantly, but there are no explicit regulations regarding volunteers under the age of twenty. Among the 100,000 men in the vanguard, 25,000 will receive firearms and sufficient military training. Ethiopia Prepares for Defense Day and Night; National Mobilization Can Reach 500,000 People; Anti-Gas Mask Drill to be Held in Addis Ababa

(London) Italy is still continuously transporting troops to East Africa, while Ethiopia is preparing for defense day and night. According to news from Addis Ababa today, the Ethiopian government will issue a general mobilization order in the coming days. Currently, there are 20,000 troops with complete equipment stationed on the border of Ogaden and Tigray. Another 300,000 unarmed soldiers carrying rifles are gathered in various strategic locations. Today, Addis Ababa, under the King's orders, will hold gas mask drills to dispel the natives' superstitions and make them understand that these protective items are not ghostly masks. (Special Telegram from the North-China Daily News, 28th)

The Ethiopian General Staff in Addis Ababa is strictly guarding the secrecy of the strength of the combat troops and the defense plans formulated with foreign advisors. However, according to well-informed sources, Ethiopia can mobilize approximately 500,000 people, but only 8% have received full military training, another 30% have received only partial training, and the rest fight on their own. However, they have also been informed of the principles of coping with close combat and avoiding air raids. The fortress of Harar, the second largest city in Ethiopia, has now been built with defense works. It is not far from the Dire Dawa station on the Djibouti-Addis Ababa railway. Ethiopian authorities claim that the garrison there, after reinforcement, has new-style anti-aircraft guns and mountain artillery units filled with ammunition, as well as 150 motorcycles. (National Telegram, 29th)

The Ethiopian government in Addis Ababa recently ordered that unemployed workers must enlist in the army or assist the Red Cross. If they are unwilling to participate in this work, they must replace it with their immortal labor to protect the country. Locals and foreigners are actively preparing for air defense to avoid air raids. However, most foreigners have either left the country or are preparing to leave the country. Vehicles loaded with luggage are passing through the capital and heading to the station. The people fear that the road protection will be insufficient, so they have purchased and stored large quantities of food. (National Telegram, 29th)

Djibouti: What kind of situation will the Djibouti-Addis Ababa railway suddenly fall into when the Italian-Ethiopian war breaks out? People are speculating about this. Most believe that this road belongs to France. Italy may not carry out aerial bombings at the beginning of the war, but when the Ethiopians use it, they will definitely bomb it. But in fact, the Ethiopian government has carried out various military defenses along the road and set up anti-aircraft guns in various places to prevent attacks by the Italian Air Force. Direct traffic between here and Addis Ababa is still obstructed. Every section must be changed once. (National News Agency Telegram, 30th)

Addis Ababa: German residents here, following the orders of the German embassy, ​​began digging large holes on the right bank of the Qabena River this morning, so that in the event of an aerial attack, German residents in Addis Ababa can hide in them. (Reuters Telegram, 20th)

Sir Frederick Dreyer Reappointed as Commander of the Armored Fleet; Promoted from Rear Admiral to Vice Admiral; Found Not Guilty in Naval Exercise Accident

(London) The government has recently issued an order that Rear Admiral Sir Frederick Dreyer will be promoted to Vice Admiral from the 31st of this month and will be reappointed as Commander of the Armored Fleet. Admiral Dreyer served as Commander of the Fleet from 1933 to 1934. When the British Navy previously held large-scale exercises off the coast of Spain on January 23 of this year, the warships HMS "Hotspur" and HMS "Renown" collided. Sir Dreyer, in his capacity as Commander of the Fleet, was charged with negligence of duty along with the captains of the respective ships. He was subsequently found not guilty by a court-martial in Portsmouth. Sir Dreyer has now been promoted to his current position. (Agence Havas Telegram, 30th)

Declaration by Four Nordic Countries; Support the League of Nations and Guarantee Peace; Four Countries Maintain Economic Cooperation

Oslo: After the foreign ministers of Norway, Sweden, Denmark, and Finland met here, they issued a declaration stating that the four countries, regarding the Ethiopian issue, intend to support all the League of Nations' efforts to guarantee peace and maintain the principles of justice and hope to handle the dispute in accordance with the League of Nations Covenant. Little Entente Conference; Three Issues Discussed; Danube River Convention Accepts Italian-French Draft; Uphold League of Nations Principles on the Italian-Ethiopian Case; Resumption of Relations with Soviet Russia to be Discussed Further in Geneva

Belgrade, Yugoslavia: The Standing Political Conference of the Little Entente countries met here yesterday to discuss the following three issues: (1) the draft Danube River Convention; (2) the Italian-Ethiopian dispute; and (3) the relationship between the Little Entente countries and the Soviet Union. Regarding the first item, the Little Entente countries are said to be accepting the draft proposed by Italy and France (this draft is based on the following four principles: (A) mutual non-aggression; (B) mutual non-interference in internal affairs; (C) agreement not to provide assistance to countries that engage in aggression without provocation; (D) in the event of a dispute, the signatory countries should consult each other). However, regarding the issue of the Habsburg dynasty's restoration, the Little Entente countries believe that this matter is of great importance, not only as an ordinary internal affair but also of international importance. It is now intended to inform France of this view through diplomatic channels. Regarding the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, the attitude to be adopted by the Little Entente countries has not yet been decided, but it will declare the necessity of adhering to the League of Nations' various principles. As for the issue of relations between the Soviet Union and the Little Entente, Czech Foreign Minister Beneš presented a report on the circumstances of his visit to Moscow in June and the signing of the Czech-Soviet mutual assistance agreement in May. According to well-informed sources, the attitude adopted by Yugoslavia towards the resumption of relations with the Soviet Union is to ascertain in advance what kind of restrictions the Soviet Union can take regarding the dissemination of communism. (Agence Havas Telegram, 30th)

Belgrade: The Little Entente foreign ministers met all day today, but no official announcement was made regarding the content of the meeting. Well-informed sources confirmed that the discussion was largely related to Yugoslavia's need to recognize Soviet Russia. Therefore, the Yugoslav Foreign Minister Stojadinović will take the opportunity to attend the next League of Nations meeting to begin negotiations with Litvinov. The proposed Danube River Convention was also discussed. Regarding this matter, a resolution has been reached, namely, that the Little Entente countries will oppose the restoration of Austria. Prince Paul of Yugoslavia invited the two foreign ministers for lunch. (National Telegram, 29th)

Remains of the Queen Transported to Brussels; Funeral to be Held on the Third of Next Month; The King Received Minor Injuries and Appeared Extremely Sad

Brussels: After the tragic death of Queen Astrid, her remains were transported back to Brussels by special train and arrived at the North Station at 8:45 this morning. The first car on the train was the hearse, followed by the sleeping car occupied by King Leopold III. In the sleeping car, those leaning on the King's side were only Prime Minister Zeeland and several cabinet members who flew to Switzerland yesterday to see the King. The King first got off the train at a small station in the Leopold district and then greeted the hearse on the platform of the North Station via a path. The King's right cheek injury was bound with bandages, and he looked extremely sad. A large number of civilians and troops lined up at the station to welcome the hearse. The civilians were silent. Once the Queen's remains arrived at the station, they were temporarily stopped at the station. (Agence Havas Telegram, 30th)

Brussels: The special train carrying the remains of the Belgian Queen arrived at the North Gate of Brussels at 8:40 this morning. The remains were transferred to a hearse and taken directly from the station to the Royal Palace, where they were placed in a small chapel. As the hearse moved forward, horns sounded mournfully. Spectators on the street bowed their heads in silence. Soldiers gathered at the Place de la Royauté and raised their guns in salute. The date of the funeral has been decided to be September 3rd. (Reuters Telegram, 30th)

Sudden Tragic News; The Whole Country is Greatly Shocked

Brussels: The tragic news of the Belgian Queen's accident by Lake Lucerne yesterday has plunged the entire country into deep sorrow. After receiving the news, the cabinet immediately convened an emergency meeting and issued a proclamation that said, "The sorrow of the former King Albert's accident still exists. Unexpectedly, this country is today mourning the Queen, who was young, compassionate, and loved by the people. The whole country is shocked and shares the King's grief. The people pay their respects to the King with loyalty and extend their deep sympathy to the Prince and Princess who lost their mother." (Reuters Telegram, 30th)

More Painful than King Albert's Own Ordeal in Recounting the Accident - The King Was Found to Have Only Superficial Injuries to His Face and Left Arm, Not Seriously Hurt; Only a Fear That His Nerves May Have Been Damaged Due to Excessive Stimulation (Havas Dispatch, 30th)

According to King Leopold, he had just replaced the chauffeur as the driver, and the Queen sat to his right, enjoying the passing scenery. They were in high spirits. Later, the King glanced briefly at a map of the road they were traveling, but in that instant, the steering wheel had turned, causing the car to crash into two trees beside the road. The accident occurred on a road twenty-four feet wide. The Queen fell beneath the first tree, her skull fractured on the right side, while the King fell beneath the second tree, it is said. According to semi-official sources, the King's car was traveling at approximately thirty to forty miles per hour. The car veered off the road and collided with a small pile of stones, then hit another pile before finally striking a tree. The Queen was thrown from the car, her head hitting the tree, resulting in immediate death. The King had a cut on his mouth and a minor injury to his left hand. An eyewitness to the aftermath of the accident told a Reuters reporter that after being thrown from the car and regaining his senses, the King immediately asked for the Queen. He was helped to where the Queen had fallen, where he knelt by her side, took her hand, and called her name. When she did not respond, the King embraced her and kissed her. Within seconds, the Queen died in his arms. The King was inconsolable, unable to speak. The King's travel passport, which was in the car, was not in his real name, as he did not want people to know his identity as the King of Belgium, to avoid unnecessary trouble. (Reuters Dispatch, 30th)

Page 8

Witness Account of the Tragedy: Jubilant Moments Unforeseen Becoming Grief-Stricken - A detective who was personally protecting the King of Belgium in Lucerne, Switzerland, recently described to a special correspondent of Havas News Agency the circumstances of the car accident. According to the report, the accident occurred at 10:15 AM, when the King and Queen were traveling in a car near Lake Vierwaldstättersee near Lucerne. The King was driving himself, with the Queen sitting beside him, and the chauffeur in the back seat. The detective and his wife were following in another car for protection. At the time, the car was traveling at a maximum speed of 50 kilometers per hour. The Queen was looking at a map, and the King turned to speak to her, when suddenly the car veered straight towards the cliff by the lake. The lakeside was heavily planted with large trees. The King seemed to want to avoid colliding with the trees, and continued driving for about fifteen meters, but unfortunately the car still hit a tree with great force, and immediately fell into the lake. The King and the chauffeur both jumped out of the car, while the Queen collapsed by the roadside, already lifeless. The King then knelt by her remains for a long time, and at 11:00 AM the remains were transported to the Haslihorn Villa in Küssnacht. Just two hours before, the King and Queen had left the villa full of joy, but in an instant, this tragic turn of events occurred. (Havas Dispatch, 29th)

The car in which King Leopold III of Belgium and the Queen were riding at the time of the accident in Küssnacht, Switzerland, has recently been recovered by locals from the reeds in the lake. The car was badly damaged; the convertible top had been torn off, and the shaft connected to the steering wheel was bent beyond recognition. The right side of the car was completely destroyed, as the driving mechanism was on the left. The left door was crushed. Local authorities have erected a cross at the site of the accident, and representatives of the Canton of Schwyz government and local officials have placed wreaths there to express their condolences. (Havas Dispatch, 30th)

Model of Motherly Virtue, Condolences Pour In from Around the World - From capitals around the world, telegrams of condolence to the Belgian royal family arrived like snowflakes. The first telegram was sent by the King of England. President Roosevelt issued a statement in Washington, saying that the Queen was a model of motherly virtue for Belgium, and that now, tragically, she had met a violent end, and the American people would share the grief of the Belgian people. Hitler said in a telegram that the sudden death of the virtuous Queen was a great loss to the Belgian royal family. The Queen Mother left Naples last night with her daughter, Princess Joséphine-Charlotte, to return home. Because the late Queen was a Swedish princess, the Swedish royal family will observe a four-week mourning period. (Havas Dispatch, 30th)

This afternoon in Beijing, members of the diplomatic corps visited the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to express their condolences. Among them, the royal families of Italy and Belgium were related by marriage, and the late Queen Astrid was also a Swedish princess, so Italy and Sweden regarded it as a national mourning, and the ceremonies were more somber. France and Belgium have a deep friendship, and after hearing the news, French President Lebrun telegraphed King Leopold and French Prime Minister Laval telegraphed Premier Pierlot to express their condolences. It is said that when the Queen's funeral is held, Laval will personally attend as a pallbearer. (Havas Dispatch, 29th)

It is reported that the Prince of Wales is now traveling from his Riviera retreat to Beijing to represent the King of England at the Queen's funeral. (Reuters Dispatch, 30th)

(Berlin) After hearing the news of the Queen of Belgium's tragic death, Prime Minister Hitler immediately sent a telegram of condolence to the King. The Führer's office, the Prime Minister's residence, and the Reichstag were all flying flags at half-mast to express mourning. (National News Agency, 29th) President Roosevelt and Secretary of State Hull today sent telegrams to the Belgian government to express their condolences for the Queen of Belgium. The President also personally telegraphed the King to express his condolences. (National News Agency, 29th)

Vatican City Pope Pius XI today telegraphed the King of Belgium to express his condolences for the Queen. The Emperor has always been a faithful Catholic, while the Queen, although born into a Catholic family, was not officially baptized until 1930. (National News Agency, 29th)

(Tokyo) Because of the passing of the Queen of Belgium, the Emperor of Japan today dispatched an imperial envoy to the Belgian embassy to express his sincere condolences to the ambassador, and will observe a fourteen-day mourning period starting on the 30th. The ceremonial officer issued a telegram of condolence. (Dentsu Dispatch, 30th)

Coping with Extraordinary Times - Japan Vigorously Seeks to Strengthen National Defense - The Army's Five-Year Plan Must Be Realized, Army Minister Hayashi Reveals Intention to Resign to Okada

(Tokyo) From the perspective of the intensification of Japan's international environment, and from the perspective of the poverty of the national livelihood and the current state of various domestic sectors related to national defense, the Army deeply feels the necessity of strengthening national defense in a broad sense. Army Minister Hayashi is determined to move in this direction and strive for its realization, and is steadily making preparations. Although the specific actions are still unclear, the key points will be a nationwide spiritual mobilization based on the stabilization of national livelihood, the development of national defense industries, the securing and control of various national defense resources, and the thorough implementation of nationalistic thought. He will present this to the government during negotiations on next year's budget, at which time Army Minister Hayashi will not only seek to implement the Army's five-year plan, but also demand that funds closely related to the stability of national livelihood be arranged to be spent so that there is no shortage. (Dentsu Dispatch, 30th)

(Tokyo) Army Minister Hayashi met with relevant agencies to study the second phase of the strategy for strengthening Army control. However, the Army Minister's own intentions are roughly as follows: (1) Declare the Army's post-meeting policy, focusing on the establishment of national defense in a broad sense and the re-recognition of national defense policy; (2) Fundamentally reform personnel administration and establish the principle of assigning the right person to the right job; (3) Correct the accumulated malpractices of various systems and customs. (Dentsu Dispatch, 30th)

(Tokyo) Army Minister Hayashi met with Prime Minister Okada on the 29th for an hour of consultations. It is reported that the content of the meeting included Army Minister Hayashi reporting on the internal situation of the military after Nagata's assassination and the results of the division commander's meeting, and informing him of his determination to resign once the incident comes to an end. Since Army Minister Hayashi has expressed an important determination, the timing of his resignation seems not far off, and it is possible that he will formally submit his resignation before the middle of next month. (Nichi-Rengo Dispatch, 30th)

The Italy-Abyssinia Case Will Likely Affect the World Naval Conference

(London) According to diplomatic sources tonight, the negotiations on the Naval Conference must wait for the results of the League of Nations Council's handling of the Italy-Abyssinia dispute on September 4 before any decisions can be made. If the Italy-Abyssinia dispute is not resolved, then any talks will be fruitless. If a dispute arises between Italy and the League of Nations, then the naval power of various countries in the Mediterranean Sea will need to be reconsidered. Therefore, diplomatic sources believe that it is not appropriate to set any plans for the date of the future naval conference stipulated by the Washington Naval Treaty. Furthermore, England previously sent a note to the Japanese government proposing to continue holding preliminary naval talks. The authorities are keeping silent on the contents of Japan's reply. However, it is generally speculated that Japan's recognition of the principle of maximum total tonnage limits is a prerequisite for participating in any naval talks. All the evidence proves this to be credible. (Note: During the London Naval Talks last year, the Japanese delegates advocated abolishing naval ratio limits and stipulating a common maximum limit for naval total tonnage to realize equal rights in naval armaments.) (Havas Dispatch, 29th)

The United States Seeks Caution in Actions Toward Russia - Deep Fear of Affecting the Far East Situation

(Washington) According to observations here today, the U.S. government's protest to Soviet Russia over the activities of the Third International is likely to affect the Far East. Secretary of State Hull met today with Undersecretary Moore, Director of the East European Division Kelley, and Director of the Far East Division Hornbeck for a long time to discuss the Soviet reply. Hornbeck's participation in the discussion indicates that any action taken by the United States may have a direct relationship with the Far East situation. The meeting ended at 6:30 PM tonight. State Department officials announced that there would be no statement on the U.S. position tonight and refused to release the State Department's opinion on the Soviet reply. (National News Agency, 29th)

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan's summer break ended, and the 26th Yuan Meeting was convened at 8:30 AM on the 30th. Sixty-nine members, including Chuan Bingchang and Chang Chang, were present, with Sun Ke as chairman and Liang Hancao as secretary-general. Matters for discussion were as follows: (1) Approval of the revision of Article 10 of the 24th Year of the Republic of China Guangdong Construction Public Bond Regulations, which was resolved and passed. The Guangdong authorities feared that the Guangdong Provincial Bank alone would not be able to handle it properly and requested that the Bank of Communications be added. (3) The Amendment to the Health Department Organization Law was resolved to be passed in accordance with the review report of the Legal Affairs Committee. This law has eleven articles, and only the first and sixth articles have been amended. The amended articles are as follows: Article 1: The Health Department is directly subordinate to the Executive Yuan and is responsible for national health affairs. Article 6: The Health Department shall have one Director, specially appointed, who shall oversee all departmental affairs and supervise subordinate officials and agencies. Gold and Silver: The London gold price remained unchanged today at 140 shillings.

Exchange Rates: In the London foreign exchange market, the U.S. dollar saw slightly increased demand this morning. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the U.S. dollar was 4 dollars, 9 angles, and 7/125, which was 25 lower than yesterday's U.S.-British closing rate. Within the first hour, it continued to fall by 1/875 to 4 dollars, 9 angles, and 6/9375. At noon, it rebounded by 0/0625 to 4 dollars and 9 angles and 7 parts. There were no further changes.

The opening rate for the British pound against the French franc was 75 francs and 13, which was one pound higher than yesterday's closing. At noon, it continued to rise by three pounds, and there were no further changes.

Cotton and Wheat: The New York cotton market opened with slightly higher prices, which it was subsequently able to maintain. Merchants are watching the effect of the cotton loan terms. Eastern buyers are not active. Cotton production in the Northwest has deteriorated before the recent rains. Many parties are paying close attention to this situation. Market sentiment is not optimistic, as it is expected that cotton farmers will sell.

Wheat: The Chicago wheat and grain market opened unchanged. Wheat prices eased in the morning due to long position liquidations, while grains tended to move upward.

A Record of the Inspection of the Disaster Situation on the Rivers

— Special Correspondent of this Newspaper, Geng Ya

From Luoyang to Kaifeng

Luoyang is a commercial center in Henan, and it was where King Wu of Zhou established his capital after conquering the Shang dynasty. During the Warring States period, it belonged to Han and was first named Guyang. Emperor Guangwu of the Eastern Han Dynasty also made it his capital. The Wei and Jin dynasties changed Luoyang to Luoyang, making it one of China's five ancient capitals. During the Shanghai war, it was once considered as a temporary capital, and the address of the National Government still exists there. The city walls are close to the Luo River, and the ground is slightly higher than the riverbed. The streets of the South Gate are directly equal to the bottom of the river, and the East Gate is also threatened by the Chan River. A few years ago, the flood submerged the large stone bridge outside the East Gate and poured into the East Street, reaching a depth of three to four feet. This autumn, the Yi and Luo Rivers experienced heavy floods, but fortunately, the city gates were not affected, while the surrounding villages were already affected by the disaster. According to investigations, the affected area is 229 square li, with 52,881 acres of land submerged and 433,350 yuan in losses. 230 houses were flooded and collapsed, and 55,400 people are awaiting disaster relief. When the reporter traveled west and arrived in Luoyang, I learned that the disaster areas are in districts four, five, and six, along the Yi and Luo Rivers. I then went to inspect. Two to three li south of the city, I reached the banks of the Luo River. The source of the Luo River is in the Mengling Mountains of Luonan County, Shaanxi. It flows southeast into Henan Province, passing through Lushi, Yongning, Yiyang, and the three counties. It enters the Yanshi border at the southeast corner of Luoyang, receiving the Jian and Er rivers. The flow rate is prone to sudden increases, carrying mud and sand, which gradually settles and raises the riverbed downstream, causing damage similar to the main stream of the Yellow River. The entire territory of Yanshi and Gongxian is submerged, which is exactly the problem of an overly high riverbed. Luoyang's terrain is flat, but not low-lying, and the embankments around the city are high and strong. When the Luo River rises, although there has been some slight erosion and overflow, after the flood crest passes, it flows back into the main channel, and there is no danger of vast stagnation. Therefore, from the southern suburbs to Longmen, that is, from the Luo River basin to the Yi River basin, the crops along the disaster-stricken areas, such as sorghum, millet, and corn, have been washed by the flood, and even lie prostrate on the ground. However, since the water has not been stagnant for long, it is easy to support them and replant. This is not comparable to a major famine.

The Yi River originates in the Dongtai'er Mountain in Lushi County, passing through Songxian and Yiyang counties, entering the territory, exiting north from Yique and entering Yanshi to the east. The nature of the water and the disaster situation are similar to the Luo River. Yique is 25 li southwest of the city, where two cliffs face each other like a gate. The east is Xiangshan, and the west is Longmen. The Yi River flows in the middle, and it was dredged by Dayu, hence the name Yique. It also has the names Quese, Quekou, Zhongshan, and other names. The Longmen cliffs are a hundred zhang high, and the walls are covered with carved stone Buddhas, numbering in the millions, solemn and magnificent, comparable to Datong and Dunhuang. The famous "Twenty Articles of Longmen" are one of the thousands of steles. The mountain caves are exquisite, and the stream water gushes everywhere. There is a famous "Gong and Drum Spring", where listening from above the spring cave, there is a sound like silk strings playing together, and gongs and drums chiming in unison. The more you listen, the more interesting and immersive it becomes. The Wei and Tang dynasties built temples in the mountains, which were rebuilt in the middle of the Qing Dynasty, named Xiangyan Quiet Realm. The flowing water, dangerous cliffs, and scenery are beautiful, but climbing is not easy. Many tourists view it from across the river from Longmen. This time, the Yi River rose and flooded the banks. The bottom layer of Buddhist caves on both sides of the cliffs was silted with mud and sand two to three feet deep. Yuwangtai and the Sprinkling Spring were also washed away, but they can be restored to their original state. However, in recent years, some foreigners have bought Buddha statues at high prices, and it is said that a complete Buddha head can fetch two to three hundred gold. The ignorant and unscrupulous people have frantically stolen them, and consequently, most of the millions of Buddha heads have been smashed. In reality, it is feared that even one out of a hundred so-called complete Buddha heads cannot be found. However, the achievements of ancient Chinese culture and art have unfortunately been almost completely destroyed, and future generations will not know what they were. This is truly an irredeemable loss. Therefore, the intention of certain foreigners to promote the purchase of Buddha heads is not to truly treasure them, but to destroy and obliterate the culture of others, which is already evident.

Returning to the city from Yique along the main road, passing Guan Gong's tomb (15 li from the city), commonly known as Guanlin, the ancient cypresses are dense, and the halls are magnificent. The tomb is behind the hall, rising like a mound. Sun Quan sent Guan Yu's head to Cao Cao, who buried it here with the rites of a feudal lord. Later generations revered and worshipped him, and this tradition has not declined over time. On the 13th day of each lunar month, and the annual Lesser Fullness solar term, villagers gather here to form a market, called "Ganjing Shisan," one to commemorate Guan Gong's single-sword assembly on May 13th of that year, and one to trade agricultural tools and living goods. That day happened to be the date of "Ganjing Shisan," and the noise could be heard from miles away. Merchants gathered from all directions and set up stalls on the spot. Some sold agricultural tools, some sold cloth, some sold groceries, some sold livestock, some sang drum operas, some told fortunes, and some sold dog skin plaster. The scene was quite similar to the temple fairs and Tianqiao street markets in Beiping. However, in the temple fairs and Tianqiao in Beiping, there are often modern young women, Western-dressed youths, and even so-called sightseers with blue eyes, who often mingle among them, and the goods sold are mostly dazzling and imported. Even the appeals of playing tricks borrow the false name of Western magic. Here, the buyers and sellers of "Ganjing Shisan" are all dressed in coarse cloth and short shirts. From a distance, they look rustic, and upon closer inspection, they are hardworking and thrifty. What is traded are agricultural products or agricultural implements, with very few urban luxury goods. Because of the recent floods, everyone wore a worried expression on their faces. Some were praying for good fortune in front of Guan Di's statue, and some were sitting on the grass, listening respectfully to books about the cycle of karma and retribution, feeling fearful and devout, and superstition seemed to deepen. This is the difference between "Ganjing Shisan" and the temple fairs in Beiping. Commerce in Luoyang is quite depressed, for the following reasons: (1) With the westward extension of the Longhai Railway, Shaanxi and Gansu can trade directly with the ports of Tianjin and Hankou, no longer passing through Luoyang as a transshipment point. (2) Frequent droughts and floods have bankrupted the rural economy, and the purchasing power of the general public is low. (3) The money market is tight, and turnover is not smooth. Although the Central Bank has a branch here, it does not redeem notes or lend money. The Henan Agriculture and Industry Bank's office charges a daily interest rate of 1.6%, which seems rather high, and it does not make loans to rural areas. The economy in the countryside is not active, and the city gates are affected by it. Therefore, more than 100 commercial firms have gone bankrupt in the past six months, and only more than 30 new ones have opened. Fortunately, former Commissioner and County Magistrate Wang Cifu abolished many exorbitant taxes and levies, reducing the burden and allowing those who have not yet collapsed to barely survive. At present, all sectors are eagerly hoping that the banking sector will come here to provide loans to help revive the agricultural and commercial economy. It is reported that the rural villages will be reorganized from district offices to district public offices, emphasizing the selection of district chiefs and increasing the power of district chiefs. The original eight districts in the county will be reorganized into five offices, which will be implemented in September, in order to carry out rural construction. If the banking sector can take advantage of this post-disaster political reform to make rural loans in conjunction, then both people and I will benefit greatly.

Returning east from Luoyang, passing through Yanshi and Gongxian, the floodwater in the fields gradually receded, but there was a lot of sand covering the land, and fertile soil had turned into barren land. If the滩地is slowly accumulated by gentle currents into new silt, it will turn into fertile land. However, if you want to sow and have a bountiful harvest, you can only wait for the coming spring. Yanshi is completely submerged, and remains untouched to this day. The proposal to relocate the seat of government, I hope, can be implemented soon, so that those of the flood victims who have the energy to spare can plan for long-term residence. The county was struck suddenly and the towns drowned. The number of the dead in the towns according to surveyors is over two hundred and thirty, including the magistrate's wife, who also perished. The disaster was so terrible that it can be expected that the number will exceed the numbers once the remains are retrieved.

As the train entered the territory of Zheng County, the eyes were finally spared from the flood. However, according to a survey, the heavy rain on July 24 caused the Wei River and Jialu River to overflow, and the affected area reached 400 square li, with houses collapsing and fields submerged, and the number of people waiting for relief was also around 20,000. The Gu Cheng Station, the site of the ancient Bi Kingdom station office, is a palace-style building, surrounded by green紗帐, with a majestic temple in the middle, with碧瓦朱壁, which looks very ancient and elegant. However, it is a small station, with only two or three passengers getting on and off. Two or three out of ten of the crops in the Jiaochang area of Zhongmou County are still immersed in shallow water, with yellow leaves and withered ears. The railroad tracks run side by side with the Yellow River, a distance of twenty or thirty li apart, the water that I had seen was rain and not from the river. The land is flat and the agricultural products are historically plentiful. Zhang Liang's hammer struck the Emperor Qin Shi Huang's Bolangsha, which is located in the north of the county bordering Yangwu County. When the train reached Kaifeng, I got off the train and entered the city. The city gate was half-open,砌with sandbags, and there were many soldiers guarding it. The atmosphere was tense, as if facing a formidable enemy. This is because of guarding the Yellow River from collapsing, because the political and economic center of the province is here.

Impressions of a Southern Journey

— Special Correspondent of this Newspaper, Qian Hua

(24) Li Pinxian's Talk

The current Director of Border Defense of the Guangxi Border and Concurrent General Director of Anti-Flooding Affairs, Mr. Li Pinxian, has been in office since 1932, exactly three full years. Mr. Li has long held military command and has profound strategic planning skills, with a reputation throughout the country. In his free time, he enjoys swimming and playing tennis, and he is well-versed in writing and calligraphy. He is uninhibited and informal, with the demeanor of a Confucian general. The reporter stayed in the Border Defense Director's office for two nights and repeatedly met and talked with Mr. Li, discussing various aspects of the southwestern border defense situation. Mr. Li said that the border defense of Longzhou was actually built single-handedly by Director Su Yuanchun. Only one-tenth of the national treasury funds were received, and nine-tenths were raised by Director Su from military pay. He loved the country and the people, and temples and shrines are all over Longzhou, and the people's praise has not waned. Later, Zheng Xiaoxu succeeded him, but with the accumulated habits of a civil official, he indulged in poetry and wine, and border affairs were neglected as a result. Since the founding of the Republic, Lu Rongting did not know what border defense was, and he did not ask about it even more. When I took over, it happened to be the outbreak of the January 28th Incident. Border affairs were tense, and the international situation was expanding. The border areas were also preparing for war. The Po Nam關was closed, and entry and exit were prohibited. Before long, the League of Nations suppressed Japan, and France shared our interests, so it made every effort to unite with us. The French Governor-General of Vietnam even invited Governor of Guangxi Huang Xuchu and I to a high-level banquet, subtly expressing the intention to resolve previous grievances, and the traffic of the 鎭南關was also restored. Since then, messengers from both sides have traveled back and forth, and there has been peace and tranquility. Regarding the unequal small details of various previous trades, they have been successively revised, and now we have reached the principle of complete equality and mutual benefit. France has a good-neighborly spirit and has a considerable understanding of our country, so there is no intention to despise us. For example, recently, when the elderly mother of Xiang Hanping was kidnapped and the bandits fled into Annam, after notifying the French side, they immediately dispatched dozens of soldiers and several armored vehicles to surround and capture the kidnappers and rescue the hostages. Another example is that when France newly promulgated the tobacco tax regulations, our merchants did not know about it in advance, and when they transported tobacco into Vietnam, they were detained and fined. After negotiating with the French side, the French negotiators said, "The fine has been submitted, and there is no way to do it except for me to take out the money myself and return it to your merchant." This is another incident. In short, diplomacy takes politics and military affairs as its backing. Only when we respect ourselves can others respect us. The Border Defense Secretary's office was built during the late Qing Dynasty, with a magnificent appearance and beautiful gardens. On the walls of the front corridor of the large hall, there is still a poem inscribed by Zheng Xiaoxu, which reads, "Falling into the southern wilderness, suddenly until today, a belly of melancholy, alone, muttering. The surrounding mountains are really what is the point, it is difficult to stop the Long River from going north." The lower paragraph says "Yiji September Xiaoxu". There are also several plum trees planted in the courtyard, and the hall is named Meizhai. It is said that Zheng was fond of 金少梅, the mother of 金月梅, but he could not get his wish from tens of thousands of miles away, so he titled the plum to quench his thirst. The old thief was lustful, as he has always been. When the reporter arrived in Longzhou, it happened that Mr. Li Pinxian had been promoted to Chief of General Staff of the Fourth Army Group. It is said that the post of Border Defense Director will be abolished, and the post of Concurrent General Director of Anti-Flooding Affairs will remain. The successor will definitely continue to work hard to ensure that border affairs are not neglected.

(25) The Majestic and Perilous 鎭南關

Among the anti-flood passes in Longzhou, 鎭南關is the most majestic and perilous, and it has the most glorious value in history. It was when the 鎭南關was attacked and broken by the French army on the ninth day of the first month of the eleventh year of Guangxu, the Guangxi governor Pan Dingxin ordered馮子材 and 王孝祺to assist. The eleventh French soldiers burned the checkpoint and retreated to Lạng Sơn. At the time our soldiers were weak and our equipment was worn out. Guangxi was shocked. 馮子材 and others vowed to exist and die with the checkpoint. The French military attacked the checkpoint on the seventh day of the second month. The situation was critical by the eighth day. General 馮, who was seventy years of age, wore short clothing and grass shoes, and holding a spear, shouted loudly and jumped on the wall and fought against the enemies. He himself cut down dozens of retreating soldiers. The three armies risked their lives and the French army was defeated. They then united with Liu Yongfu's Black Flag soldiers and chased them, defeating them at Lạng Sơn. In the last century, China suffered frequent foreign troubles and many national humiliations, the only wars in which we could raise our eyebrows were the wars at 鎭南關 and Lạng Sơn. 鎭南關belongs to 憑祥county, surrounded by high mountains and dangerous terrains. In the late Qing Dynasty, the French built a railway at 同登, which was eight li from 鎭南關. Since then, the Chinese and Vietnamese people who came and went between the borders, used 鎭南關 as a major passageway, increasing its importance. On the morning of the seventeenth, at around seven o'clock, accompanied by Mr. Dai Shaoying, the Director of Education of the Border Defence Office, I went to 鎭南關 to pay respects. The checkpoint was about 143 li from Longzhou, and the car twisted and turned into the mountain for about two hours before arriving. There was a branch office and a customs office. Mr. Huang Tinghui was a committee member and had studied in France. A native of Guangdong, he was familiar with the area. He had been in office since 1926 and was certainly a useful diplomat. The checkpoint was a few hundred steps away from the Office. There are two sets of city walls. On the outside walls are four large characters, which were written by Lu Rongting: 南疆重鎭. The inner walls are the three characters of the checkpoint, written by Zheng Xiaoxu. Because of his collaboration, the three characters of Zheng Xiaoxu have been removed. The checkpoint is located on凹of two high mountains and is not very high. Three 重砲臺were constructed at the top of the mountain to defend from above: 鎭中, 鎭南, and 鎭北. It is difficult for an army to pass. The fort on the mountains across was owned by the Vietnamese, but they were lower and in an inferior position compared to the Chinese. In touring the historically significant area, the scenes of the battles appeared before our eyes as though they were happening in the present. Our spirits were lifted in the humid heat, and we felt as if we had taken 清凉散.

(26) Government Office of the Literary 淵 District in Annam

I was able to gain a permit from the Border Defense Director and a temporary passport from Huang Tinghui. We traveled in car and there was a wooden sign that read: 安南境由此進. We presented passports at the鐵bridge because we had entered Annam. Past the bridge was the French customs. 同登belongs to the 文淵district of 諒山省, Tokyo. The government office is there. After Vietnam returned to France, 西貢 was divided into a colony and 安南， 東京， 老家， 甘埔寨 divided into protectorates. 安南still had a king and appointed officials, but the French controlled the military and administrative powers. The provinces were divided into 省九州一府, and then counties under it. 同登is a small town that is very clean with Western influence. The street signs are still in Chinese, such as 生意街. In the government office the furnishings are very similar to that of Chinese offices. There were 金字embroidered red satin that read: 世濟其美, 恩癸生佛. The district chief Yang Shaozhen greeted us in a silk hat, white 布 short shirt, long 布 pants, and拖鞋. He can speak Cantonese, French, and Vietnamese. He answered my questions thoroughly. He was a secretary for the Director of Anti-Flood and moved to be the chief. French officials were the highest with the 总督followed by 省留守使. A portrait of the emperor was hanging in the office. The official explained that the emperor was 22 and that he graduated from Paris high school 5 years ago. He was referred to as Bảo Đại and this was Bảo Đại 10 years. We also learned that 孔子was very respected in Vietnam, and that senior officials must pay respects at the temple during spring and fall. I then invited the chief to photograph. In the picture the chief had a black silk shirt, over a white shirt, with red characters that read 文淵州知州. We toured the town. There was a small school with the curriculum in Vietnamese but in French spelling. In 30 years the Vietnamese characters will be all but disappeared. There was a 中華會館 that had representatives.

武鳴之文工江塔

南寗省 government招待所門門前

Wang Kemin Returns to Beiping; Political Council Hurries to Conclude, All Departments and Sections to Finish by Month's End

Completed Economic Coordination Council Organizational Plan to Be Announced

Beiping Correspondence: Wang Kemin, Acting Chairman of the Beiping Political Readjustment Council, left Beiping for Nanjing on the 24th in response to a telegram from President Wang, to report on the political situation in North China and to discuss important official matters. Wang originally intended to travel to Moganshan, but after meeting with President Wang, he followed Wang's instructions to return north quickly, thus canceling his trip to Moganshan. He left Nanjing on the evening of the 27th and arrived in Beiping at 8:19 a.m. on the 29th. There were many people welcoming him at the East Railway Station of Qianmen. Secretary-General Yu Jiaji of the Political Readjustment Council, along with senior officials from all departments and sections, were almost all present at the station. After Wang got off the train and exchanged pleasantries with the welcomers, he immediately took a car to the East Building of the Political Readjustment Council to rest. Many guests came to visit, but Wang, due to his long journey, was unable to meet them all. He only met with Beiping Mayor Yuan Liang, Chahar Province Chairman Qin Dechun, and Beiping-Tianjin Garrison Commander Wang Shuchang separately. At around 10 o'clock, Wang personally called Secretary-General Yu Jiaji and instructed all department and section chiefs of the Political Readjustment Council to gather at the East Building for instructions. In his speech, Wang briefly described his trip south and stated that he had received a personal instruction from President Wang of the Executive Yuan to have the Beiping Political Readjustment Council conclude its work immediately. He hoped that his colleagues would complete all matters handled by the end of this month and await further instructions. After the speech, Wang left the meeting and returned to his private residence in Gali Hutong in the West City. All departments and sections of the Political Readjustment Council began their conclusion work at 1 p.m. that afternoon, and due to the limited time, they would work through the night to ensure completion by the 31st.

Wang Kemin's Remarks

After news of Wang Kemin's passage through Tianjin from Nanjing at dawn on the 29th reached Beiping, a reporter specially went to Fengtai to meet him. He was granted an audience, and according to Wang's brief remarks, "I went to Nanjing this time in response to a summons and met President Wang several times. Following Wang's instructions, I hurriedly returned north after staying in Nanjing for one night and two days. I originally intended to visit Huang (Fu) in Moganshan, but I abandoned the idea. As for the various issues discussed with President Wang, I am afraid it will be difficult to disclose them before they are implemented. The date of the sixth plenary session of the Beiping Political Readjustment Council is still difficult to predict. When the meeting is held in the future, there may not be any important cases to discuss. When I passed through Jinan last night, I met with Chairman Han (Fuju) at the station. The severity of the floods in Western Shandong is unprecedented. Han was originally scheduled to come to Beiping last night, but upon hearing that the meeting had been postponed, he decided to wait for a meeting notification before starting his journey. The North China Economic Coordination Council is mainly composed of leaders from the banking and business sectors, with the government only in a supporting role. Its organizational plan will be announced soon. Regarding the issue of navigation between inside and outside the customs, it is being handled directly by the Ministry of Communications. I have not heard anything about the progress of the negotiations or its current status. Recently in North China, in addition to the two cases of Tao (Shangming) and Liu (Zuozhou), no new issues have arisen. Minister He (Yingqin)'s stationing in the north has not been confirmed, and there is no news of Chairman Huang (Fu) coming north either. Regarding the foreign reports that Japanese industrial and commercial experts will hold meetings in Shanghai, Tianjin, and Beiping in stages, I have not received any reports on this matter, so I do not know the details." (29th)

Yixian County Magistrate Cables Request to Stop Water Obstruction in Han River – Many Houses Collapsed in Tengxian

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River has risen again, and the flooding in the disaster area is becoming more widespread. The people of Northern Jiangsu have already built two horizontal dams on Wangmu Mountain and Shengyang Mountain, extending deep into the Grand Canal. Today (28th), Yixian County Magistrate Liu Huating reported to the provincial government that the situation was serious, stating in a telegram, "Report, the Huai River Guidance Association and the laborers of Pixian County, Jiangsu, have already built two horizontal dams in the Grand Canal between Wangmu and Shengyang Mountains, extending deep into the river, obstructing the water and flooding southern Shandong and a few villages in Tongshan and Pi counties. Now, they are throwing stones and hemp bags into the riverbed between the two dam heads, intending to raise the riverbed and obstruct the downstream flow. Obstructing the water in the Han River in this way, at the expense of neighbors, disregards the lives and property of millions of people in southern Shandong and northern Jiangsu, which is truly a strange event at home and abroad. The affected people are extremely indignant and fear that they will take risks again and cause a major change. I beg you to urgently telegram the central government and the Jiangsu provincial government to strictly stop it, so as to avoid accidents. I respectfully report this, Yixian County Magistrate Liu Huating, respectfully sealed." The Tengxian County Magistrate telegraphed the provincial government to report on the recent disaster situation, stating, "(1) Blocking the railway culverts has now been completed; (2) The Chao River is still rising, and although the water from the breach west of the railway is invading eastward, the situation has eased; (3) The mountain water in Xiazhen has entered the streets, and the Grand Canal has overflowed its banks, causing many houses to collapse. We are still doing our best to protect it; (4) The water from the breach in Pei County has flowed eastward to Xiwancun; (5) The new dam at the Pengkou sluice gate has been strengthened with straw and heightened by one foot due to the mountain floods and accumulated water outside the embankment. Although it is not out of danger, it has also eased; (6) I respectfully report that I accompanied you from Lincheng back to the city and will temporarily stay to handle important official matters. I respectfully report, Tengxian County Magistrate Xie Xiwenting, respectfully sealed (28th)."

Jingqiu Railway: Jingzhe Section Surveyed and Completed

The Route is Estimated to Be 400 Kilometers Long, Requiring Construction Costs of Over 40 Million

Hangzhou Correspondence: In order to shorten the Jingguang (Beijing-Guangzhou) journey, the Ministry of Railways had previously planned to construct the Jingguang Railway. In the spring of this year, a survey team was organized, and Zheng Hua, the Chief of the Design Section of the Ministry and a representative of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, was appointed as the team leader. In May, he led more than 30 employees and departed from Beijing for the survey. After three months, the entire section has now been surveyed. Team Leader Zheng has returned to Beijing to report. It is understood that the route surveyed by the team this time goes from Nanjing through Lishui into Anhui Province, passing through Guancheng, Ningguo, Xu Xi, Huizhou, Shendu, and then into Zhejiang Province, passing through Chun'an, Shouchang, Longyou, and other places to connect with the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway. The total length is 400 kilometers, requiring a cost of 42.2 million yuan. From Longyou onwards, the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway will be fully utilized, passing through Yushan, Nanchang, Pingxiang, to Zhuzhou, and then connecting with the Yuehan Railway to utilize the southern section to reach Guangzhou. However, the Longyou to Yushan section is currently a light-weight track, so it will need to be replaced before connecting. Also, the railway from Nanjing to Xuancheng has now been built by the Jiangnan Railway Company. If this section is also utilized, the entire journey can be shortened by another half or so, and the cost can be reduced by two-thirds. The route taken by the railway goes from Beijing along the Yangtze River through Wuhu to Xuancheng, which is slightly different from the Ministry of Railways' route. It has not yet been decided whether to utilize it or build a new one. As for the future construction project, it will be completely handled directly by the Ministry of Railways to make it a state-owned railway. Once Zheng Hua reports to the Ministry of Railways, construction can be planned. (30th)

Songjiang: Liangcai Scholarship Donated to Red Cross

The local Red Cross branch recently received a letter from the Board of Directors of the Shanghai Liangcai Scholarship, along with a donation of 500 yuan and a portrait of Mr. Shi. The chairman of the association, Zhou Xuewen, stated that Mr. Shi Liangcai was born in Songjiang, was enthusiastic about public welfare, and had a well-known reputation. He was also a pioneer in the press and a pillar of the Red Cross, worthy of respect. Therefore, in the newly renovated Yilan Building of the association, a separate room was created to enshrine the meritorious members of society, Yang Liaogong, Xiang Songmao, Lei Jixing, and Mr. Shi, in a single shrine for admiration. At the same time, a letter of gratitude was sent to the Board of Directors of the Shi Liangcai Scholarship.

Suzhou: Young Man Who Failed Entrance Exam Commits Suicide

Yesterday (30th) at around 3:00 a.m., Yuan Yuchang, a patrolman from the Second Public Security Precinct, was patrolling the streets and saw a young man in Western attire holding grass paper, pacing back and forth at the entrance of Shipinong Lane inside Qimen. He asked him for questioning. The young man replied that he was going to call a doctor. Later, on his way back, Yuan Yuchang encountered him again at Xiatang under Qimen and asked if he had called a doctor. The young man replied that he was about to return home. Yuan then followed him. The young man, seeing that it was difficult to escape, pretended to point to a house in front of the Chen Ji Scissors Shop as his home and knocked on the door. The shop opened the door upon hearing the sound, and the young man immediately pushed the patrolman away and fled forward wildly. Yuan immediately gave chase. The young man ran to the riverbank and jumped into the river. At that time, there were many boats parked at the riverbank, and they helped to search, but found nothing. It was not until dawn that the body surfaced. It was then discovered that the deceased was Zhu Kun, the young owner of the Qiangsheng Milk Farm in Xinqiaoxiang, Qimen, 20 years old. He committed suicide because he failed the entrance exam for the Hangzhou Medical College. The family was notified to come to the scene, and the local court sent Luo Duzhi to inspect and coffin the body.

Wuxi: Vegetable Farmers Stop Work Collectively

The abundance of pit latrines inside and outside the city of this county is unmatched by other counties. The 25 manure firms, including Longshun and Huinong, obtained licenses from the Finance Department and organized a cooperative office in the sixth section of Guangfu Gate to guide the business of each manure firm. Since then, the buying and selling of manure fertilizer has been handled by the manure firms, and the original pit owners have found it difficult to save money, while the vegetable farmers are not free. About a thousand vegetable farmers in the city area petitioned the Party headquarters, and a few days ago, hundreds of people went to the Party and government organs to express their opposition. The Party headquarters agreed to forward the matter to the county government. The county government stated that if it is not a main road, such as the pit latrines in private gardens, they can still be bought and sold as usual. If the cooperative office is obstructing them, the vegetable farmers can report the facts to the county for verification. The vegetable farmers were satisfied and withdrew, but disturbances occurred near the cooperative office, and the lanterns were smashed. The county security team maintained order and stationed guards at each city gate to prevent accidents. At that time, the situation was tense. Feng Genfa, Zou Jinrong, and Chen Xibei, three vegetable farmers, were injured and went to the local court to examine their injuries. A few days ago, 200 to 300 manure carriers from the cooperative office also went to the county to petition, demanding fair handling. The two sides were evenly matched and could not reach a decision. Since yesterday morning, the vegetable farmers have unanimously stopped work, causing great panic among the residents. Most vegetable fields only have some thin green vegetables on the roads and in the large river pools, and the rest are salted vegetables and yellow soybean sprouts. Most of them are not produced in gardens, but the prices are extremely high. Salted vegetables and thin green vegetables are 200 yuan per catty, and yellow soybean sprouts are 160 yuan per catty. The prices of other types have also increased. After this incident occurred, County Magistrate Wang Baoxuan, in addition to ordering the police to pay attention to local security, also expressed his views on the cooperative office, saying that the government could not interfere with the vegetable farmers' strike if there were no transgressions. The establishment of the cooperative office was fundamentally illegal and should be banned. The establishment of the manure firms made it difficult for the office to exist. The current dispute was entirely caused by the monopolization of the manure trade. In the future, if the above situation occurs, their licenses will be revoked immediately, and the Public Security Bureau will be ordered to investigate strictly. In the future, the government must formulate measures for managing pit latrines, and the Public Security Bureau's First District Public Security Department will thoroughly organize and avoid disputes.

Provincial Committee Investigates Lake Fields and Completes Task

Wang Peng, Shen Jun, Chen Heng'an, members of the Finance and Construction Departments, and Qian Tangxin, a member of the Lake Field Clearance Committee, came to Wuxi a few days ago to investigate the matter of increasing the tax on lake fields. The task has now been completed. At 5 p.m. on the 30th, Wang and others went to the county government to meet with Xie Jianzhai, the head of the Second Section, to compile a list of the lake fields in the third and fourth districts and take them to the provincial government that night to report.

Changzhou: Zhencheng Road Bus Robbed Midway

The third bus on the Zhengchen Line (Zhenjiang to Jurong) of Zhengcheng Road departed from Zhenjiang Station at 9:10 a.m. on the 27th. When it reached between 11 and 12 kilometers, two bandits suddenly appeared in the bus, standing at the bus door, pulling out box guns and pistols, first shooting the driver in the leg, hitting his left leg. The bus was forced to stop, and the bandits robbed the 20-odd passengers in turn, none of whom were spared. After more than ten minutes, they got off the bus and left. Afterwards, the Zhengcheng Line Office of the Highway Administration sent personnel to investigate. The passengers lost more than 100 yuan. In addition to sending the injured driver to the hospital for treatment, the Provincial Highway Administration was telegraphed to forward the matter to the Construction Department to find a way to strictly arrest the fleeing bandits and bring them to justice. In order to prevent the bandits from using the same tricks again, the office, with the winter prevention approaching, yesterday (29th) specially wrote to the county government to forward the order to the local security team or public security substation at the ten stations from Menghe to Longhutang in Wujin County to send police to the stations at any time to inspect and patrol along the way to prevent accidents.

Hangzhou: Zhejiang Province Opens Up Autumn Silkworm Purchase

The Zhejiang Construction Department's Silkworm and Silk Control Committee, due to the smooth sales of Chinese silk in Europe and rising market prices, and the fact that the autumn silkworm season is approaching, silk cocoon merchants are very active. Silk factories in Shanghai and this province have requested to stop the monopoly and allow merchants to freely purchase cocoons to benefit the livelihood of Chinese workers. The authorities, in order to communicate with Chongqing, have divided the silkworm mulberry areas of each county into eight districts and allowed merchants to freely purchase cocoons, but merchants in this province have priority. The measures for each district have already been formulated and will be submitted to the provincial government's routine meeting next Tuesday for approval and implementation. However, according to news from cocoon merchants, the authorities intend to designate Hangzhou City and County to be purchased by Yongtai Silk Factory, and they have expressed their opposition. As for the autumn cocoon improvement fee, 1.8 yuan per dan of dried cocoons is still collected, and they are also requesting a reduction to lighten the burden on merchants and the people.

The Administrative Inspectorate of the Jiaxing-Hengzhou area will be established in the county government on September 1. Meat Industry Requests Cancellation of Education Surtax

The Jiaxing slaughter tax and surtax is 4 jiao and 5 fen per pig. Now, an additional education surtax of 1 jiao and 5 fen has been added to the tax. The meat industry is experiencing a downturn in business and is struggling to survive. The original tax and surtax were already too heavy a burden. If it is increased, it will be difficult to maintain. Currently, the Xinye Meat Industry Association and others have telegraphed the provincial and county authorities to cancel the education surtax to alleviate the suffering of the merchants.

Nantong: Opium Addicts' Factory Opens

The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Opium Commission has set up an opium addicts' factory in Xiaohai Town, Nantong, to accommodate opium addicts from the six counties of Tongzhou, Rugao, Chongming, Hai'an, Qidong, and Jingjiang to learn skills. The various departments in the factory have already started work. The hemp shoes and towels produced are sold to the area's security teams. The textiles, soap, and other products are transported and sold to the Jiangnan area. The special commissioner's office has been continuously sending opium addicts to the factory in recent days.

Ningbo: Robbery Occurs in Western Suburbs Last Night

The Maimian Bridge in the western suburbs of Ningbo has convenient transportation and a prosperous market. It is only five li from the city. Wen Xiangfu, a resident, runs the Taishan Grocery Store on the east side of the town. At around 8 p.m. on the 28th, as he was closing the door, six bandits suddenly arrived, holding pistols and flashlights, making a fierce show of force and threatening him not to make any noise. Three bandits went upstairs to search, while the other three bandits monitored Wen's actions. Soon, the three bandits carried down a box from upstairs, broke it open, and stole 200 yuan in banknotes, 95 yuan in cash, and more than 200 jiao in small change. After the robbery, they fled towards Banlu'an. After the robbery, the victim immediately reported it to the Huangulin Public Security Sub-bureau and the Bailongwang Temple Police Station to apprehend them. By the time the police team arrived, the bandits had gone far away and could not be caught.
