Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

### A Tame Sheep? Or a Porcupine?

— Chui

Mussolini's recent posture towards Abyssinia has the air of burning his boats, using the strength of a lion to hunt a rabbit, and wiping them out in one fell swoop. Indeed, although Abyssinia has the advantage of terrain and popular support, after all, it is a small country, how can it withstand the latest airplanes and cannons trampling on it? The demise of Abyssinia was long expected by us.

Unexpectedly, there is a rumor in Abyssinia recently that "Mussolini will capture a tame sheep, but unexpectedly encounters a porcupine." Tame sheep? Porcupine? This question remains to be considered by us and proven after the event. Although Abyssinia is known as the Black Lion Kingdom, compared to the great powers, it is still a sheep, but this sheep cannot be considered a tame sheep, it can only be considered a merino sheep. Because the King of Abyssinia has repeatedly declared that he would rather be a shattered jade than a complete tile, that is, even with one soldier and one arrow, he would still resist to the end, this sheep can be considered extremely stubborn.

Even in terms of military use, Abyssinia has many high mountains, deep forests, and deserts, so it is quite inconvenient to use troops against it, and it is also very closely related to the interests of Britain. Therefore, even if this war does not expand, given the fierce nature of the Abyssinian people and the incompatibility of the soil and water, and the obstacles of high mountains and deep forests, it will not be easy to wipe them out in one fell swoop. In case the war expands or even triggers a second world war, then the tame sheep and the porcupine are really somewhat unpredictable.

But now the arrogance of the imperialists is extremely high, even bombs are not taken to heart, and a mere porcupine is not worth mentioning. However, if this kind of doctrine spreads, the plunder of colonies will become the highest purpose of the country, completely becoming a world where the strong eat the weak, and what you sow is what you reap, and those who accumulate evil causes will inevitably bear the consequences one day. After the European War, after the pain subsided, they once thought of Eastern civilization, but they gradually forgot over time, and a second world war is about to break out again.

But the great powers are after all the great powers. Not long ago, Mr. Mo made a strong declaration, saying that if anyone prevented the movement to use troops against Abyssinia, I would subdue them by force. However, according to a report from Rome yesterday, Italy expressed that it did not want to sever ties with the League of Nations and would declare that it would respect Britain's rights, and France also opposed sanctions against Italy and expressed satisfaction with the Italian government's intention to present Italy's reasons at the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting on September 4. If this is the case, the great powers have shown signs of compromise, and I think in this situation, Abyssinia should just be a tame sheep, why be a porcupine? It is true that a clever person does not suffer losses in front of him, the words of the ancients are not bad at all.

### Home Life

— Cheng Quan

In my youth, holding books in the spray of morning sunlight, in the clear sunlight of the evening, in the winding tones of a contralto singing "Home, Sweet Home," I often dreamed of having a home: so light, so gentle and beautiful, like a small dream on a midsummer night, so quiet, peaceful, and comfortable, like a bird's nest, and finally, so happy, innocent, and bright like the Garden of Eden; where, in my home, a loud and clear laugh would always bloom, like an evergreen tree always green in the garden.

Such a pile of cloud-like, ethereal, and beautiful dreams, following my ever-broken, uncollectible life, has been going on for many, many years (yes, in retrospect, it is an unimaginably long period)! Now, I have lost the happiness of reading Shelley's lyric poems under the moonlight on the third or fifteenth night, and in the exhaustion of running around to obtain some broken and ruined life, I have lost my youth, lost the loud laughter of my youth, lost the fantasias as beautiful and hazy as moonlight; however, I have begun to have a home!

It is a real, truly my own home!

(Friends—those who already have homes—patting my shoulder, half like a malicious threat, half like a well-intentioned warning, and in fact it is a person who has been through it all boasting and teasing a "newcomer," loudly saying, "Good fellow, you finally have a home too. Good, grab it tightly, don't let it give you a headache, frown, or even cry, that's a good fellow! That……"

"Go to hell!" I so exaggeratedly, with confident and proud, very rude and loud words answered them.)

So, I really had a home.

Home, it is really such a home! I carry it heavily day by day: day by day, I also see it more, understand it—understand many, many things, those that are not in the fantastic dreams of my youth, and cannot be found in the song "Home, Sweet Home" that moves the hearts of people all over the world!

For a person who has already crawled over the weight of having a home, this point may not be very unfamiliar: at the beginning and end of the month, I sweat uncomfortably over the rent, firewood, and rice; so, those domestic routines begin to attack you. Like me, my wife is also a person with future ideals and a considerable plan for life; but unfortunately, that ideal is many times higher than mine (one), and this plan is too far from reality. So, living in this low-level life that is so strongly discordant with ideals, she is always (almost determined to be) a gloomy companion; so, when I bring a tired brain home from the office in the evening, that row of books on the bookshelf almost becomes a hateful mockery to me, and now I am not enjoying Shelley's lyric poems, but the endless recitation of my wife's hysterical ideals, which, like a thousand sharp needles, holds my heart tight; I feel uncomfortable, I scold her loudly, I will simply go crazy!

But, that "plan," that "ideal," that negotiation, was the most beautiful poem to me in the beginning (yes, didn't we tirelessly talk for three days about the style of a sideboard?)

As the days passed, we had children! The child interrupted, which was a terrible thing for me! But what made my wife most happy! Without feeling tired, she talked to me all night about the merits and demerits of books like "Infant Care Method" and the merits and demerits of milk powder brands. She said twelve kinds of milk powder names in one breath.

I was angry and tired, turned over, yawned, and closed my eyes.

So a terrible voice rose: "What? I've been talking for so long, aren't you listening?"

"I am listening, dear!" So, I reopened my eyes, abandoned the recollection of being insulted by the manager for a word missing on a document during the day, and began to listen to her narrating the strengths and weaknesses of "Le To Jing"……

So, I finally lived day by day. I will not forget that I still have a broken and ruined life.

However, I have a home……

Yearning

— Hua Zhi

It is autumn, a season for yearning!

In the morning, draped in my morning robe, I push open the south-facing window. The sunlight, like a lazy dog, falls wearily onto the old, paint-faded floor of my bedroom. It seems to be searching for a resting place, having lost the authority it held during the clamorous days of cicadas.

The sky is high, and sluggish clouds drift east and west. The morning breeze greets my face, and I cannot help but shiver. After all, it is autumn, and I am a middle-aged man approaching the twilight of my life!

Across from my bedroom is someone's garden, with a vermilion church blocking my view. The cross on its top glitters with ostentatious lights. Yes, for three years, it has stood before me every day, arrogant and unchanged in its normal state: whether in the peach-blossomed, seductive spring, or the morning glory-draped summer, or in the snow-filled winter, it remains aloof and independent. But I know that the garden's new owner once wanted to tear it down and build a lotus pond, because its old owner's glorious history was erased by a transaction two months ago. Next autumn, thinking that the church might be stripped of its religious authority, I will not be able to live here much longer.

Thinking of this, I inexplicably think of home. That home is in the distant north, now a dusty ancient city buried by yellow sand. I have an elderly grandmother who likes to wear a bright red pomegranate flower beside her silver temples. She told me the reason: the pomegranate flower in full bloom symbolizes a flourishing scene. In the back garden of my house, there are five pomegranate trees, planted by my great-grandfather. His intention was that pomegranates are symbols of many children. Liking pomegranates means hoping for many sons and grandsons, which is largely the same as my grandmother's reason. However, these five pomegranate trees did not understand the good intentions of their master's cultivation. Although they bloomed with red flowers every autumn, the family declined day by day. I have a young uncle who, after I left home, was beaten out of the house by my grandmother with her cane because he lost money gambling and wanted to change the family name of the house with the five pomegranate trees. Speaking of descendants, I should be responsible for my great-grandfather's hopes, but at the age of thirty, I have not yet married a wife. In my old grandmother's letters, she tirelessly tells me about the issue of my family's lineage. Should I find a wife soon? I hope tonight, I can have a lighthearted dream: I return to my ancient hometown with my young wife, and my grandmother, leaning on her cane, points to the blooming pomegranate trees and says in a frighteningly joyful voice, "This year, the pomegranate flowers will bear even more pomegranates!" Yes, an old woman with a full head of white hair wants to see the next generation of children and grandchildren!

Looking at the cross of the church, I hope it is as healthy as my old grandmother; I also hope that its new owner will let it stand there forever as a lovely decoration. It has always been so proudly unchanged in its attitude, and it can withstand the frost, snow, and harsh cold of winter!

Dusk at the Ancient City Wall

— Hua Ling

Gradually moving from the bustling streets through the desolate alleys, heading north, we ran all the way to the outskirts, and the sky was slowly darkening. In the open wilderness, an ancient city appeared before us. The city walls had no battlements; from afar, only a tall wall remained. On the dilapidated city head, newly sprouted wild grass covered the surface. A few idlers wandered about, evoking a touch of ancient sentiment in the tranquil dusk. Occasionally, two or three idlers held birdcages, squatting on the city wall, waiting for sunset, waiting to pass the day. Some children flew kites here to while away the evening. All of this subtly mocked the ancient city.

Unconsciously, we ran onto the city wall, hoping to catch a glimpse of ancient Yangzhou from atop. Who knew that the dusk on the city wall would evoke a different kind of emotion. The sun had already set on the desolate outskirts outside the city, and evening dew covered the vast forests. Only the edge of the sky was tinged with egg-yolk colors. An ancient atmosphere perfectly painted the outline of the ancient city, creating a harmonious feeling. From the distant wilderness road came a faint sound of bells, causing wandering eyes to gaze afar. A line of small mules had disappeared into the vast twilight. The gentle breeze carried the fading sound of ding... ding..., as if this was a unique sound of the ancient city.

Looking west, the sun cast its last rays, precisely outlining the high spires of some large temples. This enticement quickened our pace. We descended the city wall, crossed the city bridge, and walked west along the river. There, a group of people were getting into rickshaws in front of a temple. Peeking in the doorway, everyone exclaimed in unison: "This is the Shi Kefa Shrine and Cemetery!" It turned out that the protagonist of the fiery tragedy of the "Ten Days of Yangzhou" was hiding so desolately and quietly in an inconspicuous place outside the city of Yangzhou. Behind the shrine should be Plum Blossom Ridge. Seeing the desolate state of the shrine, it must have been buried in overgrown weeds for quite some time, forgotten by people. But now, people are putting a glorious coat on it again; many workers are moving bricks, tiles, and wood, and people are rediscovering old tastes!

Leaving the shrine, we headed west in search of the large temple. In the dimness, a tall archway appeared before us, inscribed with "Tianning Zen Temple." It turned out that the Tianning Temple in Yangzhou was also unexpectedly discovered. Feeling our way into the temple gate in the twilight, we immediately felt a sense of vastness and seclusion, as if we were thrown into a deep valley, our hearts hovering, unsure where to attach themselves. Beside a silent flight of stairs, the Kangxi Imperial Stele Pavilion was built, slightly making up for an empty corner. Beyond the front hall, there was another empty flight of stairs, leading to the Great Hero Hall? Everything was desolate and quiet. We ran through it without encountering a single monk. Passing through the Great Hero Hall, we ran straight to the back, where a tall Sutra Library stood erect. However, we could not pass through a closed hall door. A sense of emptiness forced us to retreat. On the way back, we realized that the managers of this empty, large temple were not monks but crows. The courtyard was covered in crow droppings, and the trees were filled with black crows and nests. Circling this empty courtyard were not the sounds of Qingqing and Hongyu, but the cawing of crows. The crows reflected the desolation of the temple, yet the crows replaced the liveliness of the temple. I dared not run in the courtyard, but only rubbed the inscriptions on the walls of the long corridor as I darted out of the temple gate. At this moment, a heavy bell suddenly rang at the end of the corridor. The bell rang, but my companions ran out with laughter. Here there is still a bell, it is only regrettable that the bell sound is too lonely.

A Snack

— Especially

We, this group of young porters, all share a love for mountains.

It is precisely because of this love that the shapes of mountains and water, as they enter our eyes, are instinctively perceived as uniquely charming, shaking our hearts and bursting with joyful elation.

The mountain path is not lonely. Besides our group, the air does not allow it to remain quiet, perhaps stirring up a layer of solemnity that exceeds its due tranquility.

If you are about to climb over a mountain pass, there are often many bells ringing, and along with the sound of bells, there are the hooves of horses. This immediately gives you a shock, subconsciously making you think of unpleasant things. In this way, the faces from old novels constantly flood your mind, such as "After the sound of hooves, bandits emerged, with the leader holding a steel knife, thick eyebrows, and coarse eyes," or "From afar, one heard a burst of bells, faintly mixed with shouts, rushing straight towards us." These kinds of stories circulate in your mind. Although the aforementioned stories are all elusive, given the current situation, they are liable to occur.

In fact, when the bells and hooves appear, there are no burly men, nor thick eyebrows and coarse eyes. It is just a few donkeys carrying some supplies, stumbling along. Behind them are drivers weathered by wind and rain. Probably because the "responsibility" has been lifted, they wear a light joy on their faces, saying something, a Red Peach brand cigarette hanging from their lips, smoke rising and forming a cloud ring.

The donkey stopped, releasing greenish-yellow excrement, steam rising from it.

——Where to eat breakfast?

——Over there, let's pull the rope, they went over there.

Page 21

People are just so hopeless, with particularly strong responsiveness. As soon as they hear someone say "eat breakfast," their own stomach immediately starts to rumble, as if it would be good to eat something right away. Calculating, it has only been two or three hours since breakfast this morning. Why is that? I don't understand.

——Let's have a snack, I suggest.

The head porter did not object, perhaps thinking in his heart, "Why be in such a hurry?" But he didn't dare to say it, burying it in his stomach. From the hesitant expression that was revealed, it could be seen.

——At Yangjia Street ahead!

It's decided. We walked, silent, each with our own thoughts hidden in our hearts.

Yangjia Street is not very big. The straight road is somewhat S-shaped. We unloaded our luggage in front of the thatched-roofed houses, and the long wooden benches were quickly occupied by us.

——Serve a bowl of shuifan (rice in water) and some tofu pudding.

The porters and companions all separated, each concerned with their own food. Lao Huang, Tie, and I were at the same table. Because we ate a lot, the boss's legs never stopped moving.

——Another 300 cash worth of sweet potatoes.

——Sold out, sir. The boss's daughter came over, smiling: Have another bowl of tofu pudding?

The daughter was about twenty years old. Because of insufficient nourishment, the greenish color on her face could not be hidden, but her active energy was always charming.

——Can the one cooking rice fry two eggs? Lao Huang continued.

——Unless it's market day, you can't buy eggs here. She laughed again.

——What else? You go find some? Buy them, and I'll fry them.

She walked out with the money, leaving behind a silent desolation at this table.

——Let's go, it's not early! The head porter called out, urging us.

We donned our luggage, and we were back on our way. Looking at Lao Huang, he wore a bitter face——

——Why hasn't the young lady come back yet? He was probably thinking this.

Radio Highlights

The Chinese Children's Story Broadcasting Society, in response to requests from all walks of life, will broadcast the world literary work "Sans Famille" daily, scheduled to complete in two months. The society uses correct and fluent Mandarin, and tells stories with theatrical techniques, creating a new type of art in the broadcasting world. It is also equipped with appropriate music (undertaken by those with experience in stage effects) to seek the realism of the story, there are generous and tragic songs (twelve new songs have been written), there is beautiful and moving music (a music team is formed, totaling five people). During this Children's Year, the Society specially presents this most intelligent spiritual feast to hundreds of millions of children, and to all parents and teachers in the world.

The art lecture hall founded by artist Mao Zhizhong, broadcasted on Shanghai Radio for the previous two semesters, and was praised by audiences from various ports. The summer vacation was suspended for three months. Now it is autumn, and it is heard that it was invited by Mr. Chen Zhengzhang, director of the Aerospace Radio Station, to be broadcasted on the station, from September 9th, daily from 2:45 PM to 3:30 PM, and publish Chinese and Western painting scores for art to meet the needs of the audience, to supplement the lack of teaching in the previous two semesters. The printing fee is 20 cents per volume of Xiaoyang, in order to popularize more prints, a special advance sale is offered for only one dollar of Dayang, and stamps are generally discounted by 10%. Those who want to order should hurry.

The Yuguang Society is led by Mr. Zhang Hui, the singing director of the former Great Natural Singing Group. It has broadcasted special programs on Wu Lei Terrace, and has been praised by ladies from all walks of life. Now, due to being hired by the Shanghai Municipal Charity Water Disaster Amusement Association, it has agreed to perform singing as a guest appearance on stage in the New World on September 2. Please pay attention to people from all walks of life. (Farmer)

Mr. Yuan Suju, director of the Greater World Chinese Radio Station, in order to make its internal programs more exciting, in addition to the original Shen Xue, Jiang Zhu, Jin Chenggui and other programs, now especially invites the Tianyun Southern Opera, which has won countless audience praises on the radio, to broadcast Male and Female Cups on the station daily from 9:45 PM to 10:30 PM. It is heard that the internal artists include Xu Qinyan, Chen Weiliang, Zhang Pengfei... etc., all of whom are outstanding talents from all over the sea.

Since the Shanghai Yuanchang Radio Station published various song scores, it has been well received by all walks of life. Now I hear that the radio station has published "Sweet Song Collection" priced at six cents, and "Parrot Collection" priced at three cents. The contents are all kinds of popular songs on the market. The stock of books is about to be sold out, especially the members of various singing groups. Recently, they have been buying from the radio station one after another. The address is No. 7, Sanrangfang, Caishi Road, Shanghai.

Movie News

New Era Landscape

— Xiang

"Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside" has as many as 5,000 feet of exterior scenes shot in Su. After being washed out by the production department, the light is clear, the scenery is quiet and beautiful, and the results are very satisfactory.

The re-examination of the script for "Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside" has been approved, and the review committee has exceptionally awarded it: "This script's humorous tone exposes the evils of local bullies and has a good connotation. The re-examination is approved and should be properly captured and produced to achieve perfection." This shows the review committee's emphasis on the script.

Little Ah Yuan Ms. Huang Naishuang sang the "Rice Planting Song" from "Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside" at the recreation fair in Lafei Garden some time ago and was very popular.

The "Rice Planting Song" is the handwriting of a famous composer, the lyrics are brisk, and the song is beautiful. In response to Baidai's request, she will go to the company tomorrow to harvest the record. It is expected that when it is released in the future, it will definitely become popular for a while.

Paris Theater Opens Today

The entire renovation is completed, and the theater is brand new

The Paris Theater on Xiahui Road has recently spent a lot of money to renovate the theater, beautify the colors of the walls and paint in the theater, and replace all the telephones in the theater with the latest models. The sound machine and projector have also been improved so that the sound and light aspects are all excellent. In addition, the seat prices have been re-set with the aim of economization. All the renovations have been completed, and the theater will be opened today (Saturday), selecting and showing the United Artists giant production "Resurrection". The film stars Aina Stein and Frederick March. When it was screened in Nanjing and other theaters, it was more popular than all other films. It is expected that today, on the side of Zhaolong Road, there will be a new atmosphere of crowded traffic.

Yueming Prepares a Drama

Drama is showing a trend of resurgence at the moment, because drama is a valuable art. Although the public's appreciation is currently weak, it will eventually be recognized by the public one day. Now, in addition to independently established drama groups, various film companies also have drama groups. Yueming Film Company has also been actively preparing a drama group recently, and has already built a drama stage in a corner of the huge photography studio. As for the candidates in charge, it is heard that Wan Laitian, the director of Nora, who was publicly screened in Jincheng and won unanimous praise from the audience, and Jinshan, who successfully played the role of Krelock lawyer in Nora, will jointly take the responsibility.

Gift of "Peach Blossom Fan" Songs

Xinhua's "Peach Blossom Fan" has two famous songs in the famous songs, one is "Love Song" and the other is "Sweetness of the Wedding", which have already been printed and distributed to all walks of life. The songs were sung in every household and became popular for a while. Recently, 100,000 more copies of the songs have been printed to meet the needs of song lovers. Regardless of whether they are local or foreign, anyone who sends two cents of postage to the Propaganda Department of Xinhua Company, 3rd Floor, Gong Stage, Aiduoa Road, Shanghai, will be sent the original team. The two songs were written by Ouyang Yuqian and composed by Liu Xue'an. After admiring them, Baidai Company has contacted and cut the films on the previous day. From now on, there will be two more great works in the wax film, which will be broadcast on the radio before the screening of "Peach Blossom Fan".

Experimental Troupe Participates in Flood Relief Fundraising

Performing Moliere's "The Miser"

The Experimental Troupe has decided to participate in the Flood Relief Fundraising Society on the evenings of September 1st and 2nd, at the Amusement Fair held in the New World, to perform the French playwright Moliere's famous five-act drama "The Miser". It is currently busy rehearsing. Participants include Ms. Yuan Peipei, Cao Fang, Fang Pei and others, as well as Liu Hengzhi, Pan Gongliang, and all the students of the Teaching and Experimental Institute. The director is Liu Yawei.
